/**
33 
 * <p>QR Codes can encode text as bits in one of several modes, and can use multiple modes
34 
 * in one QR Code. This class decodes the bits back into text.</p>
35 
 *
36 
 * <p>See ISO 18004:2006, 6.4.3 - 6.4.7</p>
37 
 *
38 
 * @author Sean Owen
39 
 */
40
